（106學年度入學新生適用）**

**International Program in Electrical and Communication Engineering for Bachelor at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Compulsory Courses**

**(Applicable to Newly-Admitted Students of 2017.)**

106.01.18 一○五學年度第三次教務會議通過

Passed by the 3st Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on January 18, 2017

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on April 26, 2017

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on June 21, 2017

Except English (I) and English (II), Students are required to obtain 6 credits from 3 different thematic courses before graduation. The “English Testing” course is provided to students who fail to score 350 in a TOEIC mock held in the end of their first academic year. They will need to take the exam again after the course and pass; otherwise, they will need to take another “English Testing” course next semester.</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育<br/>Physical Education<br/>（0）</p></td><td><p>體育<br/>Physical Education<br/>（0）</p></td><td><p>體育<br/>Physical Education<br/>（0）</p></td><td><p>體育<br/>Physical Education<br/>（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★通識教育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>Courses</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分，其餘2學分學生可自由選擇，由通識講座課程、微課自主學習或通識四大領域課程中選課。</p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>The General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a two-credit course from each category to get eight credits before graduation. The rest two credits can be chosen from the General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit and Self-Study course or four categories upon their needs. </p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in English.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="7"><p>★</p><p>專</p><p>業</p><p>基</p><p>礎</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Basic Compulsory Courses </p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>括弧內數字為學分數。<br/>Parenthesized numbers are course credits.</li><li>畢業學分：128學分 (通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分)。<br/>Required credits for graduation: at least 128 credits (The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.)</li><li>必修學分：87學分 (包含共同必修：23學分、通識教育科目：10學分、專業基礎必修科目：54學分)。<br/>Required credits:87 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 23 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses 54credits.)</li><li>專業中階選修(入門引導)：至少18學分。<br/>Intermediate Elective Courses: at least 18 credits.</li><li>專業進階選修：至少 6學分【電機系研究所之科目】。<br/>Advanced Elective Courses: at least 6 credits (the courses offered by the institute of Electrical Engineering)</li><li>其餘選修：17學分。<br/>Free elective credits: 17 .</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含共同必修科目4學分、通識教育科目10學分及專業基礎必修科目54學分、中階選修3學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from University Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 54 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 3 credits from Intermediate Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.  </li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題。<br/>The experiential learning courses: Graduation Project.</li><li>海外實習每學期可取得9學分，可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修學分，但必須繳交實習心得報告並經審查合格。<br/>Oversea internship each semester can obtain 9 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The credits have to be evaluated according to the required report of the internship prepared by the students.</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering. </li></ol></td></tr></table>

**International Program in Electrical and Communication Engineering for Bachelor at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Compulsory Courses**

**（Applicable to Newly-Admitted Students of 2018.）**

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2017, on May 2, 2018

108.01.02 一○七學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2018, on January 02, 2019

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2018, on May 01, 2019

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Approved by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 6, 2020

-Python and Fundamental Computer Programming -C are two 2-credit courses, according to the college requirement, which have to be completed before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation. Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 54credits.)</li><li>專業中階選修(入門引導)：至少18學分。<br/>Intermediate Elective Courses: at least 18 credits.</li><li>專業進階選修：至少6學分【電機系研究所之科目】。<br/>Advanced Elective 19.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含共同必修科目4學分、通識教育科目10學分及專業基礎必修科目54學分、中階選修3學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from University Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 54 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 3 credits from Intermediate Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題(EI302)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project (EI302) is a three-credit compulsory course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented Courses."</li><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>海外實習每學期可取得9學分，可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修學分，但必須繳交實習心得報告並經審查合格。<br/>Oversea internship each semester can obtain 9 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The credits have to be evaluated according to the required report of the internship prepared by the students.   </li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、行動裝置應用程式開發(EI308)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計 (EI408)、人機互動概論(EI318)本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Mobile Device Application Development (EI308), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Human-Computer Interaction(EI318) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.)</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3 版)／102.04.19 修訂

**List of Compulsory Courses**

**（Applicable to Newly-Admitted Students of 2019.）**

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2018, on May 01, 2019

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Approved by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 6, 2020

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。其餘2學分學生可自由於四大領域課程中選課。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation. The rest two credits can be chosen from four categories upon their needs.</p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in numbers are course credits.</li><li><strong>畢業學分</strong>：128學分 (通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。)<br/>Required credits for graduation: at least 128 credits (The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.)</li><li><strong>必修學分</strong>：85學分 (包含共同必修：21學分、通識教育科目：10學分、專業基礎必修科目：54學分)。<br/>Required credits: 85 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 21 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 54credits.)</li><li><strong>專業中階選修(入門引導)</strong>：至少18學分。<br/>Intermediate Elective Courses: at least 18 credits.</li><li><strong>專業進階選修</strong>：至少6學分【電機系研究所之科目】。<br/>Advanced Elective Courses: at least 6 credits (the courses offered by the institute of Electrical Engineering)</li><li><strong>其餘選修</strong>：19學分。<s><br/></s>Free elective credits: 19.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含共同必修科目4學分、通識教育科目10學分及專業基礎必修科目54學分、中階選修3學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from University Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 54 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 3 credits from Intermediate Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外實習每學期可取得9學分，可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修學分，但必須繳交實習心得報告並經審查合格。<br/>Oversea internship each semester can obtain 9 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The credits have to be evaluated according to the required report of the internship prepared by the students.   </li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、行動裝置應用程式開發(EI308)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計 (EI408)、人機互動概論(EI318)本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Mobile Device Application Development (EI308), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Human-Computer Interaction(EI318) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.)</li></ol></td></tr></table>

**List of Compulsory Courses**

undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation. The rest two credits can be chosen from four categories upon their needs.</p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in numbers are course credits.</li><li><strong>畢業學分</strong>：128學分 (通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。)<br/>Required credits for graduation: at least 128 credits (The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.)</li><li><strong>必修學分</strong>：85學分 (包含共同必修：21學分、通識教育科目：10學分、專業基礎必修科目：54學分)。<br/>Required credits: 85 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 21 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 54credits.)</li><li><strong>專業中階選修(入門引導)</strong>：至少18學分。<br/>Intermediate Elective Courses: at least 18 credits.</li><li><strong>專業進階選修</strong>：至少6學分【電機系研究所之科目】。<br/>Advanced Elective Courses: at least 6 credits (the courses offered by the institute of Electrical Engineering)</li><li><strong>其餘選修</strong>：19學分。(選讀外系課程，不包含通識教育及共同必修)。<s><br/></s>Free Elective Courses: at least 19 credits from departments other than this program, excluding General Education Courses and University Compulsory Courses.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>必修課程初次修課(停修不算)須在本班修讀始予承認。<br/>The first-time registration (excluding course withdrawal) is limited to ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含共同必修科目4學分、通識教育科目10學分及專業基礎必修科目54學分、中階選修5學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from University Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 54 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 5 credits from Intermediate Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、行動裝置應用程式開發(EI308)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計 (EI408)、人機互動概論(EI318)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Mobile Device Application Development (EI308), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Human-Computer Interaction(EI318) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.)  </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

Implementation-oriented courses"<s> </s></li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python(EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.) </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含共同必修科目4學分、通識教育科目10學分及專業基礎必修科目54學分、專業選修31學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from University Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 54 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 31 credits from Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302)為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業進階選修及其餘選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Advanced Elective Courses and the Free Elective Credits. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309) 、人機互動概論(EI318)、深度學習使用Python(EI320)、電動載具技術(EI326)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計 (EI408)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python (EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.)  </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

(II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="14"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★</p><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="14"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。通識跨域課2學分，學生可自由於四大領域課程中選課。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.General Education Interdisciplinary Course 2 credits can be freely chosen by students from any of the four categories</p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General Education Courses taught in English.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年<br/>(Academic (包含共同必修：17學分、院必修：4學分、通識教育：10學分、專業基礎必修：50學分)<strong><br/></strong>Required credits: 81 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 17 credits; College Compulsory Courses: 4 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 50 credits.)</li><li><strong>專業選修</strong>：至少28 學分。<br/>Elective Courses: at least 28 credits.</li><li><strong>自由選修</strong>：至少19學分(不包含通識教育及共同必修)。<s><br/></s>Free Elective Courses: at least 19 credit, excluding General Education Courses and University Compulsory Courses.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>必修課程初次修課(停修不算)須在本班修讀始予承認。<br/>The first-time registration (excluding course withdrawal) is limited to ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含院必修4學分、通識教育10學分及專業基礎必修50學分、專業選修66學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from College Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 50 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 66 credits from Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>須通過大學程式能力檢定 (Collegiate Programming Examination, 簡稱CPE) 累計二題始得畢業；或取得Amazon (AWS)、Google、Microsoft雲端證照者，「基礎級」證照（無論張數）僅能折抵一題，其餘進階證照一張折抵一題。</li></ol><p>There are two avenues to meet the graduation requirements on programming skill.</p><p>1. The students could take the Collegiate Programming Examination (CPE) and pass at least two CPE questions in a cumulative manner during their undergraduate study.</p><p>2. The students could earn Amazon (AWS), Google, or Microsoft cloud certifications. The foundational certifications (regardless of the number of certifications the student owns) can be applied in equivalence to only a single CPE question while other advanced certifications can be applied in a one-to-one equivalence to the CPE questions.</p><ol><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業選修12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Elective Courses. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、人機互動概論(EI318)、深度學習使用Python(EI320)、電動載具技術(EI326)、半導體元件模擬實驗(EI332)；高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計(EI408) 、演化計算(EI415)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python (EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326) , Semiconductor Device Simulation Lab. (EI332), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits  (EI408) , Evolutionary Computation (EI415) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.)  </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。<br/>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> 英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★</p><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。通識跨域課程，學生可自由於四大領域課程中選課。<br/>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. 3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註Remarks</p></td><td colspan="16"><ol><li>括弧內數字為學分數。<br/>Parenthesized numbers are course credits.</li><li><strong>畢業學分</strong>：<strong>128學分</strong> (通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。)<br/>Required credits for graduation: at least 128 credits (The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.)</li><li><strong>必修學分：81學分 </strong>(包含共同必修：17學分、院必修：4學分、通識教育：10學分、專業基礎必修：50學分)<strong><br/></strong>Required credits: 81 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 17 credits; College Compulsory Courses: 4 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 50 credits.)</li><li><strong>專業選修</strong>：<strong>至少28學分</strong>。<br/>Elective Courses: at least 28 credits.</li><li><strong>自由選修</strong>：<strong>至少19學分</strong>(不包含通識教育及共同必修)。<s><br/></s>Free Elective Courses: at least 19 credit, excluding General Education Courses and University Compulsory Courses.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>必修課程初次修課(停修不算)須在本班修讀始予承認。<br/>The first-time registration (excluding course withdrawal) is limited to ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含院必修4學分、通識教育10學分及專業基礎必修50學分、專業選修 69學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from College Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 50 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 69 credits from Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>須通過大學程式能力檢定 (Collegiate Programming Examination, 簡稱CPE) 累計二題始得畢業；或取得Amazon (AWS)、Google、Microsoft雲端證照者，「基礎級」證照（無論張數）僅能折抵一題，其餘進階證照一張折抵一題。</li></ol><p>There are two avenues to meet the graduation requirements on programming skill.</p><p>1. The students could take the Collegiate Programming Examination (CPE) and pass at least two CPE questions in a cumulative manner during their undergraduate study.</p><p>2. The students could earn Amazon (AWS), Google, or Microsoft cloud certifications. The foundational certifications (regardless of the number of certifications the student owns) can be applied in equivalence to only a single CPE question while other advanced certifications can be applied in a one-to-one equivalence to the CPE questions.</p><ol><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業選修 12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Elective Courses. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、人機互動概論(EI318)、深度學習使用Python(EI320)、電動載具技術(EI326)、半導體元件模擬實驗(EI332)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計(EI408)、演化計算(EI415)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python(EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326), Semiconductor Device Simulation Lab. (EI332), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Evolutionary Computation(EI415) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.) </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。<br/>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。<br/>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 電機通訊學院英語學士班 必修科目表
International Bachelor Program in Electrical and Communication Engineering for at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2025）**

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

114.12.24一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on December 24, 20255

The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). regulations.</li><li>必修課程初次修課(停修不算)須在本班修讀始予承認。<br/>The first-time registration (excluding course withdrawal) is limited to ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含院必修4學分、通識教育10學分及專業基礎必修56學分、專業選修 63學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from College Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 56 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 63 credits from Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>須通過大學程式能力檢定 (Collegiate Programming Examination, 簡稱CPE) 累計二題始得畢業；或取得Amazon (AWS)、Google、Microsoft雲端證照者，「基礎級」證照（無論張數）僅能折抵一題，其餘進階證照一張折抵一題。</li></ol><p>There are two avenues to meet the graduation requirements on programming skill.</p><p>1. The students could take the Collegiate Programming Examination (CPE) and pass at least two CPE questions in a cumulative manner during their undergraduate study.</p><p>2. The students could earn Amazon (AWS), Google, or Microsoft cloud certifications. The foundational certifications (regardless of the number of certifications the student owns) can be applied in equivalence to only a single CPE question while other advanced certifications can be applied in a one-to-one equivalence to the CPE questions.</p><ol><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory 3 credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業選修 12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Elective Courses. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、人機互動概論(EI318)、深度學習使用Python(EI320)、電動載具技術(EI326)、半導體元件模擬實驗(EI332)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計(EI408)、演化計算(EI415)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python(EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326), Semiconductor Device Simulation Lab. (EI332), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Evolutionary Computation( EI415) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.) </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。<br/>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。<br/>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> 英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>★</p><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。通識跨域課程，學生可自由於四大領域課程中選課。<br/>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation. General Education Interdisciplinary Course 2 credits can be freely chosen by students from any of the four categories</p><p>通識教育科目10學分，須選修英語授課課程。</p><p>These five courses admitted must be the General (通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。)<br/>Required credits for graduation: at least 128 credits (The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.)</li><li><strong>必修學分：81學分 </strong>(包含共同必修：17學分、院必修：4學分、通識教育：10學分、專業基礎必修：50學分)<strong><br/></strong>Required credits: 81 credits (University Compulsory Courses: 17 credits; College Compulsory Courses: 4 credits; General Education Courses: 10 credits; Basic Compulsory Courses: 50 credits.)</li><li><strong>專業選修</strong>：<strong>至少28學分</strong>。<br/>Elective Courses: at least 28 credits.</li><li><strong>自由選修</strong>：<strong>至少19學分</strong>(不包含通識教育及共同必修)。<s><br/></s>Free Elective Courses: at least 19 credit, excluding General Education Courses and University Compulsory Courses.</li><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。<br/>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</li><li>必修課程初次修課(停修不算)須在本班修讀始予承認。<br/>The first-time registration (excluding course withdrawal) is limited to ones offered by this program.</li><li>英語授課課程以「★」表示，包含院必修4學分、通識教育10學分及專業基礎必修50學分、專業選修 69學分。潛在英語授課課程以「☆」表示。<br/>「★」：The credits granted by English-taught courses include 4 credits from College Compulsory Courses, 10 credits from General Education, 50 credits from Basic Compulsory Courses, 69 credits from Elective Courses. 「☆」: The potential English-taught courses.</li><li>終端學習課程：畢業專題<br/>The experiential learning courses：Graduation Project.</li><li>須通過大學程式能力檢定 (Collegiate Programming Examination, 簡稱CPE) 累計二題始得畢業；或取得Amazon (AWS)、Google、Microsoft雲端證照者，「基礎級」證照（無論張數）僅能折抵一題，其餘進階證照一張折抵一題。</li></ol><p>There are two avenues to meet the graduation requirements on programming skill.</p><p>1. The students could take the Collegiate Programming Examination (CPE) and pass at least two CPE questions in a cumulative manner during their undergraduate study.</p><p>2. The students could earn Amazon (AWS), Google, or Microsoft cloud certifications. The foundational certifications (regardless of the number of certifications the student owns) can be applied in equivalence to only a single CPE question while other advanced certifications can be applied in a one-to-one equivalence to the CPE questions.</p><ol><li>修習「普通物理實驗」、「電子電路實驗(一)／(二)」等3門課程者，必須通過該課程所規定之儀器檢定項目。<br/>Students who study the General Physics Lab., Electronic Circuits Experiment (I), (II) must pass their required tests for instrument operation.</li><li>畢業專題(EI302))為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. <br/>Graduation Project (EI302) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</li><li>海外交換學習每學期，最多可折抵專業選修 12學分，但海外所修課程必須屬於電通工程，認抵需依本班規定辦理。<br/>Oversea exchange studying each semester can offset maximally 12 credits of the Elective Courses. The accepted credits of the courses taken oversea have to be related to the electrical and communication engineering, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by this program.</li><li>邏輯電路實驗(EI108)、超大型積體電路設計導論(EI309)、人機互動概論(EI318)、深度學習使用Python(EI320)、電動載具技術(EI326)、半導體元件模擬實驗(EI332)、高階數位IC設計(EI407)、微感測器及感測電路設計(EI408)、演化計算(EI415)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本班或外系修習)。<br/>Logic Circuit Lab. (EI108), Introduction to VLSI (EI309), Human-Computer Interaction (EI318), Deep Learning with Python(EI320), Electric Vehicles Technology(EI326), Semiconductor Device Simulation Lab. (EI332), High-Level IC Design (EI407), Design on Micro-Sensor and Sensor Circuits (EI408), Evolutionary Computation(EI415) are courses of “Digital Application Courses.” Students are required to pass at least two “Digital Application Courses.” (Students may take these courses from other department.) </li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。<br/>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。<br/>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。<br/>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

3. 必須修畢至少**30學分**，才予承認其輔系資格。

An individual student who minors in this Program must take courses mentioned above up to 30 credits or more before he/she can have the minor admitted.

註 Notes：

1. 必修科目共計**18學分**，必須修習本班認可之**英語授課科目**才予承認。

The compulsory courses offered by this program must be taken at least 18 credits.

2. 選修科目必須修習本班認可之**科目**才予承認。

The elective courses must offered by this program.

3. 必須修畢至少**27學分**，才予承認其輔系資格。

An individual student who minors in this program must take courses mentioned above up to 27 credits or more before he/she can have the minor admitted.
